```mermaid
classDiagram
  class CanonicalEvent {
    +setAuthorizer(authorizer)
    +setBody(body)
    +setHttpMethod(method)
    +prepare()
    +toAwsEvent()
  }
  class Authorizer {
    +setUsername(username)
    +syncFromAuth0()
    +setSolutions(solutions)
    +setOrganizationId(id)
  }
  class DictionaryToObject {
    +__init__(dict)
  }
  class update_entity {
    +lambda_handler(event, config)
  }

  CanonicalEvent --> Authorizer : uses
  update_entity ..> CanonicalEvent : receives event
  DictionaryToObject <-- update_entity : passed as config
  Authorizer <|-- Authorizer : instantiated
  CanonicalEvent <|-- CanonicalEvent : instantiated
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
  participant Script
  participant File as entitiesToArchive.csv
  participant AuthorizerObj as Authorizer
  participant EventObj as CanonicalEvent
  participant Updater as updateEntity.lambda_handler
  participant DTO as DictionaryToObject

  Script->>File: open(filename) and readlines()
  Script->>File: iterate each line
  Script->>AuthorizerObj: Authorizer().setUsername(...)\n.syncFromAuth0()\n.setSolutions(...)\n.setOrganizationId(18)
  Script->>EventObj: CanonicalEvent().setAuthorizer(...)\n.setBody(...)\n.setHttpMethod(...)\n.prepare()
  Script->>Script: split line, trim ids
  Script->>EventObj: setPathParameters(solution_id, entity_id)
  Script->>Updater: call lambda_handler(event.toAwsEvent(), DictionaryToObject(...))
  Updater-->>Script: returns result
  Script-->>Script: loop next line or finish
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> Idle
  Idle --> FileOpened : open file
  FileOpened --> Reading : readlines()
  Reading --> Processing : for each line
  Processing --> PreparingAuthorizer : create authorizer
  PreparingAuthorizer --> PreparingEvent : create event
  PreparingEvent --> InvokingUpdate : set path params\ncall lambda_handler
  InvokingUpdate --> Processing : continue loop
  Processing --> Done : no more lines
  Done --> [*]
```
